# <a name="archived-release-notes-for-monthly-channel"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-103">每月通道的封存版本資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-103">Archived Release notes for Monthly Channel</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-104">這些版本資訊可提供 Office 365 專業增強版、Visio Pro for Office 365、Project Online 電腦版用戶端以及 Office 365 商務版的每月通道更新所含新功能和非安全性更新的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-104">These release notes provide information about new features and non-security updates that are included in Monthly Channel updates to Office 365 ProPlus, Visio Pro for Office 365, Project Online Desktop Client and Office 365 Business.</span></span>

 > [!NOTE]
>- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-105">我們通常會在一段時間每個月推出功能 (有時甚至推出修正程式)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-105">We often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Monthly over a period of time.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-106">如果您現在沒有看到如下所述的項目，您可以預期它近期會推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-106">If you don’t see something described below right away, you can expect it soon.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-107">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-107">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/when-do-i-get-the-newest-features-in-for-office-365-da36192c-58b9-4bc9-8d51-bb6eed468516)
>- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-108">現有 Office 365 專業增強版安裝上的 Microsoft Teams - 從 7 月初開始，對 Office 365 專業增強版 (和 Office 365 商務版) 的更新將包含 Microsoft Teams。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-108">Microsoft Teams on existing installations of Office 365 ProPlus - Beginning in early July, updates to Office 365 ProPlus (and Office 365 Business) will include Microsoft Teams.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-109">新增 Teams 的日期取決於您使用的更新通道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-109">The date when Teams will be added depends on which update channel you're using.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-110">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[隨著 Office 365 專業增強版部署 Microsoft Teams](https://docs.microsoft.com/DeployOffice/teams-install)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-110">Please refer to [Deploy Microsoft Teams with Office 365 ProPlus](https://docs.microsoft.com/DeployOffice/teams-install) for additional information.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-115">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-115">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-116">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-116">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-117">這項變更透過利用軟體轉譯避免特定 Intel 圖形驅動程式發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-117">This change circumvents a problem with certain Intel graphics drivers by leveraging software rendering.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-118">我們修正了樞紐分析圖的右鍵功能表，以啟用 [顯示詳細資料] 選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-118">We fixed the right click menu for Pivot Charts to enable the option to Show Details.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-119">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-119">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-120">解決造成網頁增益集存取數位版權管理郵件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-120">Addresses an issue that caused web add ins to access Digital Rights Managed messages.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-125">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-125">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-126">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-126">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-127">**輸入會傳回多個值的公式**：現在您可以快速輸入公式來傳回多個值，並且值會自動溢出至相鄰的儲存格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-127">**Type a formula that returns multiple values:** Quickly type a formula that returns multiple values, and they'll automatically spill into the neighboring cells.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-128">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-128">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/5c2c9cbb-def8-409a-b380-2fbf91b20aa3)

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-129">**六個功能強大的函數：** 我們新增了六個新的函數，讓您的試算表功能更強大：FILTER、SORT、SORTBY、UNIQUE、SEQUENCE 和 RANDARRAY。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-129">**Six powerful functions:** We’ve added six new functions to supercharge your spreadsheets: FILTER, SORT, SORTBY, UNIQUE, SEQUENCE and RANDARRAY.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-130">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-130">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/003df6c7-1dcb-4388-8e2e-0fe77a0887bc)

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-131">**資料視覺化工具增益集：** 從 Excel 快速建立 Visio 流程圖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-131">**Data visualizer add-in:** Quickly create Visio flowcharts from Excel.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-132">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-132">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/bee3b5aa-aaaf-4401-acc6-276b711c763c)

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-133">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-133">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-134">**改善共同撰寫：** 改善共同撰寫的體驗，盡可能讓其他人即時收到修改過的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-134">**Coauthoring improvements:** Improved the coauthoring experience by making it more likely that content changes will be received by others in real time.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-137">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-137">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-138">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-138">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-139">修正 Microsoft Access 中的「更新查詢」執行時或在 SQL 中使用 UPDATE 陳述式時，可能導致發生錯誤「查詢已損壞」&quot;&quot;的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-139">Fixed an issue in Microsoft Access that may cause the error &quot;Query is Corrupt&quot; when an Update Query is run, or an UPDATE statement is used in SQL.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-140">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-140">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-141">從不受信任的網路共用編輯受保護的檔案時，Excel 可能會發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-141">Excel may have issues when editing a protected file from an untrusted network share.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-142">解決在未開啟活頁簿時，搜尋最近使用的檔案會造成當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-142">Resolved an issue that may have caused a crash when searching for recent files while no workbook is open.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-143">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-143">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-144">解決會導致使用者在嘗試從 [帳戶建立] 內容連絡支援服務時，看到具有 [確定]&quot;&quot; 按鈕的空白訊息方塊的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-144">Addressed an issue that caused users to see an empty message box with an &quot;OK&quot; button when trying to contact support from the Account Creation context.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-145">在 2019 年使用巴西時區時，週期性會議和約會以 2020 年的錯誤時段顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-145">When using the Brazilia time zone in the year 2019, recurring meetings and appointments are displayed in the wrong timeslot for the year 2020.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-146">此變更與設定使用巴西時區的用戶端或設定使用該時區的會議和約會相關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-146">This change is relevant for clients set in the Brazilia time zone or for meetings and appointments set in that time zone.</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-147">解決會導致使用者在開啟 [規則] 對話方塊時看到「在這部電腦中建立的規則和 Microsoft Exchange 上的規則衝突」提示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-147">Addressed an issue that caused users to see a &quot;The rules on this computer do not match the rules on Microsoft Exchange&quot; prompt when opening the Rules dialog.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-148">修正 SMIME 演算法選取的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-148">Corrected an issue with SMIME algorithm selection.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-149">解決會導致會議中的 [位置] 欄位意外更新的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-149">Addressed an issue that caused the Location field in meetings to get updated unexpectedly.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-150">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-150">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-151">解決 Office 更新可能會非預期地從 Office CDN 而不是預期使用的來源 (例如本機或網路共用或 Configuration Manager 提供的位置) 下載檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-151">Resolved an issue where Office updates may have unexpectedly downloaded files from the Office CDN instead of the intended source, such as a local or network share, or Configuration Manager-provided location.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-152">修正 ODT 和 GPO 更新期限設定中的問題，在其中，相對期限只有在第一次設定時才會有效，此修正可啟用後續更新的相關期限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-152">Fixed an issue in ODT and GPO Update Deadline setting where relative deadline only works the first time it is set, the fix enables the relative deadline for subsequent updates.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-179">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-179">Feature updates</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-180">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-180">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-181">**建立更易於存取的 PDF：** 建立 PDF 檔案，在儲存之前，協助工具檢查程式會指出應該修正的協助工具問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-181">**Create more accessible PDFs:** Create a PDF and the accessibility checker will point out accessibility issues to fix before you save.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-182">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-182">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/064625e0-56ea-4e16-ad71-3aa33bb4b7ed)

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-184">**將敏感度標籤套用至您的文件和電子郵件**：將敏感度標籤套用至您的檔案和電子郵件，使其符合組織的資訊保護原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-184">**Apply sensitivity labels to your documents and emails:** Apply sensitivity labels to your files and emails to keep them compliant with your organization's information protection policies.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-185">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-185">Learn more</span></span>](https://aka.ms/officemipdocs)

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-189">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-189">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-190">**建立更易於存取的 PDF：** 建立 PDF 檔案，在儲存之前，協助工具檢查程式會指出應該修正的協助工具問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-190">**Create more accessible PDFs:** Create a PDF and the accessibility checker will point out accessibility issues to fix before you save.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-191">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-191">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/064625e0-56ea-4e16-ad71-3aa33bb4b7ed)

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-251">**Outlook 中的 [插入連結] 功能表會插入含有租用戶系統管理員所定義的權限的連結：** Outlook 中使用 [插入連結] 所插入的連結，只有具有連結權限的使用者可使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-251">**Insert Link Menu in Outlook will insert a link with permission defined by tenant admin:** A link from the Insert Link MRU in Outlook would insert a link that only worked for users who already had permissions to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-252">這常會造成使用者來回傳送電子郵件，要求對方授與文件的存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-252">This often caused back and forth emails between users asking to be granted access to a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-253">我們已更新這項體驗，現在插入的連結將具有由租用戶系統管理員設定的預設權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-253">We've updated this experience so now the link is inserted with the default permission set by the tenant admin.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-254">**Outlook 視覺更新**：這是 Outlook 核心體驗的視覺更新的一部分，其中更新 [讀取窗格] 和 [檢查] 中的 [郵件訊息] 版面配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-254">**Outlook visual refresh:** This is part of the visual refresh of core experiences in Outlook, updating how mail messages layout in the reading pane and inspector.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-255">**共用行事曆更新的速度更快：** 針對 Office 365 中的共用行事曆，Outlook 可以使用 REST API 更新這些行事曆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-255">**Shared calendar updates just got faster:** For shared calendars in Office 365, Outlook can update these calendars using the REST API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-256">開啟預覽以更快且更可靠地更新共用行事曆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-256">Turn on the preview for faster and more reliable updates to shared calendars.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-257">**在搜尋結果中查看相關郵件：** Outlook 會分析搜尋字詞，然後在搜尋結果的最上方顯示最相關的電子郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-257">**See relevant messages in your search results:** Outlook analyzes search terms and shows the most relevant email messages at the top of your search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-258">您也可以在 [最佳結果] 區段中查看依日期排列順序的所有結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-258">You'll also see all results sorted by date in the Top Results section.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-259">**傳送郵件給正確的人員：** 只需按一下 [收件者：] 行，然後從 [建議的連絡人] 中選擇。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-259">**Send the mail to the right person:** Just click the To: line and choose from suggested contacts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-260">圖片和目前狀態指示器可協助您選擇正確的人員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-260">A picture and presence indicator helps you choose the right person.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-261">**抵禦攻擊的進階防護：** 使用 Office 365 進階威脅防護，您會受到保護，不受電子郵件主旨、附加的郵件、簽署的郵件、網路路徑內超連結的攻擊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-261">**Advanced protection against attack:** With Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection, you're protected against attacks through hyperlinks within email subjects, attached messages, signed messages, network paths, and so on.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-262">**在不同燈光下查看郵件：** 使用太陽/月亮按鈕以在讀取窗格中於淺色和深色背景之間切換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-262">**See your messages in a different light:** Use the Sun/Moon button to switch between light and dark backgrounds in the reading pane.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-263">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-263">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/3e2446e0-9a7b-4189-9af9-57fb94d02ae3)

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-357">**聯結類似欄位上的表格：** 在比較合併表格的欄位時，取得及轉換 (Power Query) 現在具有近似文字比對邏輯 (也稱為模糊比對)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-357">**Join tables on similar columns:** Get & Transform (Power Query) now features approximate text matching logic (also called fuzzy matching) when comparing columns for merging tables.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-358">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-358">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/ffdd5082-c0c8-4c8e-a794-bd3962b90649)

We also added a sort by Flag to make it easier to find flagged items. Finally, Focused Inbox has a better interaction model with search: Focused Inbox remains until a user starts to search and we show 'Results' text shown after a search completes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-p248">**Outlook 增益集警告：** 有時 Outlook COM 增益集會發生問題，讓其餘 Outlook 功能變慢。這些問題可能是因為以下的事件延遲：在 Outlook 資料夾之間進行切換、新的電子郵件送達、開啟行事曆項目等等。當這類問題發生時，Outlook 會在通知列中顯示警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-p248">**Outlook add-in warnings:** Occasionally an Outlook COM add-in can encounter problems that slows down the rest of Outlook. These problems could be due to latency of events such as switching between Outlook folders, arrival of new emails, opening Calendar items, etc. When such issues arise, Outlook will display a warning in the notification bar.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-p249">**從 Outlook 提醒對話方塊加入小組會議：** 當 Outlook 提醒使用者有即將來臨的會議時，如果即將來臨的會議是小組線上會議，則它會顯示 [線上加入] 按鈕。這個動作與從 Outlook [提醒] 對話方塊加入商務用 Skype 會議的體驗類似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-p249">**Join Teams meetings from the Outlook Reminders dialog:** When Outlook reminds users of an upcoming meeting, it will show a Join Online button if the upcoming meeting is a Teams online meeting. -   <span data-ttu-id="eaaa3-1157">**取消選取儲存格：** 在工作表中進行選取，並取消選取不小心按到的儲存格而不必重新開始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eaaa3-1157">**Deselect cells:** Make selections in your worksheet and deselect cells that you accidentally clicked without having to start over.</span></span>
